(Havas dispatch, 30th)

(Paris) French aviator Trouillet, the aviation advisor to the Abyssinian Emperor, is currently in Sendosel, Italy. He told a Rome correspondent of the Morning Post yesterday, "The rumor that the Abyssinian Emperor has already boarded a British plane and fled to British Kenya, and that I am traveling to that place to escort the Abyssinian Emperor to another location is not true. I have been ordered to fly to the location of the Abyssinian Emperor and, if necessary, plan to escort the Abyssinian Emperor to the French Riviera in southern France. The Abyssinian Emperor will never surrender to the Italian army, but at the last moment, he may agree to retire to France." (Havas dispatch, 30th)

British House of Lords Discusses Effectiveness of Sanctions Against Italy 24

(London) Diplomatic official Stanhope declared in the House of Lords today that if the line of sanctions against Italy can be maintained for a long time, he believes that Italy will realize that its position is far less advantageous than not resorting to force. Stanhope made this statement in response to a motion by Member Davies advocating that the League of Nations should, in accordance with the methods of the Lytton Commission of Inquiry, appoint a commission of inquiry into the Italian-Abyssinian dispute. Stanhope also firmly stated that sanctions against Italy are gradually taking effect. If we can prove that the war is fruitless, then we will achieve something that no one needs to be ashamed of, and that will have a deterrent effect in the future. The British government cannot agree with Davies' motion because it is impractical and unsound. Davies then withdrew his motion. (Reuters dispatch, 29th)

(London) During today's meeting of the House of Lords, Lord Davies proposed that the League of Nations should follow the precedent of the Lytton Commission of Inquiry and send a commission of inquiry to Abyssinia to conduct an on-site investigation. Lord Stanhope, Under-Secretary of State for Foreign Affairs, responded on behalf of the government, saying, "The League of Nations was unable to threaten Italy with sanctions to avoid war before the outbreak of the Italian-Abyssinian War, and was also unable to stop it after the war broke out. All of this is true. However, the current war has not yet ended, and the Italian army is making progress, leading to it being further and further away from its base. The difficulties it encounters are also increasing day by day. This is what we should know." (Havas dispatch, 29th)

(Rome) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs recently submitted a report on the Ministry's budget to the Chamber of Deputies, which detailed the origins of the Italian-Abyssinian dispute and analyzed the attitude adopted by the British government, stating, "Since the Franco-Italian agreement was concluded on January 7 of last year, before the British House of Commons held its general election (the event in November of last year), the British policy had already changed its direction. What is the reason for this? It will become clear in the future. Italy had already stopped raising requests to amend the distribution of mandated territories. However, Abyssinia's serious threat to the safety of Italy's East African colonies made Italy's development towards Abyssinia a matter of course. It is inappropriate for other countries to come out and block it, especially since Britain and France have encompassed all the mandated territories in the world, but want to hinder Italy's future. Is there any reason for this in terms of morality, law, or history?" The report also said, "The League of Nations' condemnation of our country's actions is actually a legal trick. It is appropriate for us to ignore it and not ask about it, even if it lasts for a hundred generations." (Havas dispatch, 29th)

Germany Denies Annexation of Austria; Austria Mobilizes Troops; Prevents Major Events 26

(Berlin) A person from the Prime Minister's Office told a Reuters interviewer yesterday that there was no basis for the rumors that Germany was making military preparations in the western Austrian border area. He said that the Ministry of National Defense had recently guaranteed that there would be no extraordinary events in southern Bavaria this year. In addition, a large detachment of riflemen is currently conducting a ten-day exercise in Garmisch, and another 80 army sports leaders are participating in training in the Bavarian Alps. The peacetime troops currently stationed in Bavaria are indeed more numerous than during the period when compulsory military training was heavily enforced, but there is no extraordinary concentration of troops there. (Reuters dispatch, 30th)

(Berlin) Foreign reports that Germany is preparing to occupy Austria by force have aroused great resentment here. Semi-official sources say that these reports are "malicious and clumsy tricks to poison the political atmosphere," and that these rumors "can prove that the sole purpose of the German government is to build peace in foreign policy and advocate amity in the European political situation, but in other respects, there are some authorities who want to create an atmosphere that plunges the political situation into turmoil." (National Telegram, 30th)

(Vienna) According to well-informed sources here, the reason why the Austrian government transferred troops from Vienna and the east to the western provinces of Salzburg and Tyrol is that there is a risk of serious events occurring at any time in the current European international situation, so it is making preparations in advance. The rumors circulating that the troop movements were caused by an incident involving the Tyrol Home Guard are dismissed by the authorities as unfounded. There are currently 5,000 troops stationed in Tyrol, 80% above the normal number. In addition, two battalions of Styrian infantry have arrived at the town of Ried in Upper Austria, near the German border. British Cabinet Meets with Labor Unions to Discuss German Issues; List of Issues to be Presented Soon 27

(London) The cabinet held a meeting at 10:00 AM today and submitted the British government's list of issues regarding the German memorandum for discussion. It is generally believed that this list of issues will be submitted to the German government. (Havas dispatch, 30th)

(London) The British cabinet today considered the questions to be submitted to Germany, hoping to gain a clearer understanding of certain points contained in the German memorandum. This document still needs to go through another cabinet meeting before it can be sent out. It is likely that it will be submitted to Germany tomorrow or Saturday. The signatories of the Locarno Pact previously proposed a solution to the West European situation to Germany, to which Germany responded. Its memorandum contained a general outline of a new peace plan. There seems to be no difference of opinion between Britain, France, and Belgium regarding the content of its questions. It is reported that Foreign Secretary Eden advocates drafting the questions in his own way, meaning that the questions raised by Britain will be moderate and constructive, but there should be no doubt about the points that Britain wants to clarify. It is generally known that the British questions will be largely the same as those speculated on April 24th, except that the colonial issue will not be raised, which is still undecided. It is likely that Britain will ask: Is Germany willing to modify the League of Nations Covenant before rejoining the League of Nations? Does Germany recognize the status of Danzig and Memel and the independence of Austria? Does Germany agree to include the declaration of a West European "sky agreement" in the negotiation of an air force limitation treaty? Is Germany willing to conclude non-aggression treaties with its eastern neighbors, but also recognizes the right of these countries to conclude mutual assistance agreements with their neighbors? Does Germany refuse to unilaterally abrogate treaties in the future? (Reuters dispatch, 30th)

(London) The list of questions that the British government should raise regarding the German memorandum of March 31st was finalized by Foreign Secretary Eden last night. After being approved by the cabinet tomorrow, it will be sent to Sir Phipps, the British ambassador to Germany, for transmission to the German government. Foreign Secretary Eden intends that this list of questions be issued as soon as possible so that the German government can submit its answers before the meeting of the League of Nations Executive Council on September 11th. It is generally known that the questions raised by Britain have no threatening nature, but only ask Germany to explain its true intentions on the following points so as to facilitate the mediation work, such as: Regarding the League of Nations, will the League of Nations Covenant be separated from the Treaty of Versailles as a separate issue? Regarding the issue of West European security, will the bilateral non-aggression pact proposed by Germany be incorporated into the collective security mechanism? Cabinet members have fully agreed on the wording of the list of questions, but it has not yet been definitively decided whether the colonial issue should be raised. In addition, according to reliable sources, the Polish Chargé d'Affaires in Britain recently stated to Foreign Secretary Eden that issues purely involving Polish-German relations should not be included in the list of questions. It is also reported that Soviet Ambassador Maisky also explained to Eden that Germany's views on East European security must be explored, but according to semi-official sources, Britain does not intend to include this issue in the list of questions. (Havas dispatch, 29th)

(London) When Prime Minister Baldwin answered a question from a member of parliament yesterday, he said, "The government has never considered the issue of transferring any mandated territories to other countries, nor is it discussing it at present." This is inconsistent with the actual situation learned by our reporter. According to our reporter, colonial experts have recently conducted in-depth research on how Britain can make concessions to Germany on the colonial issue without harming the interests originally maintained by the British Empire. The conclusions are as follows: The Tanganyika region (formerly belonging to Germany and now mandated to Britain by the League of Nations) runs through North and South Africa and occupies a key strategic position. Its military and economic relations are extremely important and cannot be transferred to Germany. British territories in East Africa, such as Kenya, Northern and Southern Rhodesia, and Tanganyika, have similar characteristics and cannot be transferred to Germany. As for the parts of Southwest Africa that originally belonged to Germany, they are now governed by the Union of South Africa, which has long expressed its opposition to the transfer of jurisdiction. Britain should not overstep its authority. Therefore, the only colonies that Britain can consider transferring are Nigeria, the Gold Coast, and Sierra Leone in West Africa. Generally speaking, there should be no difficulties in transferring Nigeria and the Gold Coast to Germany. Germany was originally a major customer of the products produced in these regions, and it can be allowed to develop its influence there. The transfer proposal has symbolic significance, which is used to appease people so that the movement to revise the treaty will lose momentum. However, in view of the recent active activities of Germans in Southwest Africa, the country's former colony, people are deeply concerned that after the country restores its power in Europe, it may take violent actions in Africa, which is quite worrying. South African Minister of Defense Biro recently proposed a plan to strengthen national defense in Congress, which is nothing more than taking precautions. (Havas dispatch, 29th)

Hungarian Revolution: A Fleeting Moment; Table Knives as Weapons; Nothing More Than a Farce 28

Beijing: The so-called "Sickle and Hammer" movement initially seemed like a major political movement, but the result was just a farce. The leaders of this movement claimed that they would occupy the capital on May 1st, which was just empty talk. The beginning of this movement was due to the fact that after several failed elections, István Bús Szametz, a right-wing radical member of the Hungarian party, set up another banner to compete. His party members were all farmers and unemployed young people. In the past few weeks, they had several secret meetings. Bús armed his party members with private property and secretly trained them for military action, preparing for an uprising on May 1st. However, the police got wind of it first and arrested its leaders and ninety party members yesterday, imprisoning them behind bars. The so-called "weapons" of the party members were nothing more than "table knives," and the so-called uniforms were nothing more than military officer's coats purchased from old stores. The police also found that Bús still calls himself a "poet." (National Telegram, 30th)

Burial of the Late King of Egypt: Solemn and Reverent Ceremony; New King Returns Home from London 29

Cairo: The burial ceremony of the late King Fuad was held today with solemn rites. Egyptian cavalry gathered in the palace square first. As the ceremonial cannons fired, sailors from the royal yacht moved the royal coffin from Abdeen Palace to a gun carriage, drawn by six black horses. At this time, planes soared in the sky, and the carriage proceeded to the burial site in the Al-Rifa'i Mosque. The onlookers were as thick as a wall, and silent. According to ancient rituals, seven cows were slaughtered on the street to share the meat among the people. The procession was two miles long. In addition to the royal family, the dignitaries included the entire cabinet and members of the diplomatic corps. While the burial ceremony was being carried out here, a grand commemorative parade was also held in Alexandria, with ten thousand participants. All trams and shops were brightly lit in accordance with Egyptian customs. (Reuters dispatch, 30th)

Cairo: The late King Fuad I was buried in the Al-Rifa'i Mosque today. The mausoleum in the hall was built under the supervision of the late king during his lifetime. Early this morning, thousands of mourners lined up between Abdeen Palace and the mosque. Several huge tents were set up in the gardens of Abdeen Palace to accommodate guests. At 10:30, Palace Minister Shirfika led the palace officials out of the palace on foot. Several sailors also carried the coffin out on their shoulders and placed it on a gun carriage. The mourners were silent and did not make any noise. Then the procession began to move forward, heading straight to the Al-Rifa'i Mosque cemetery. (Havas dispatch, 30th)

The World Celebrates Labor Day Today 30

(Paris) May 1st is the 50th Labor Day. The origin of this festival in the world originated in the United States. The American Labor Congress held a meeting in Pittsburgh in 1881 and proposed the "three-eight system" (eight hours of work, eight hours of education, and eight hours of rest), and designated May 1st of each year as Labor Day. Five years later, in 1886, the first Labor Day commemoration was held, and it has been followed as an example every year since. Due to its influence, it has become popular in various countries. The French labor organization has traditionally been divided into two factions: the General Confederation of Labor and the Unified General Confederation of Labor. By March of this year, they merged into one, called the Unified General Confederation of Labor, and will hold the first congress in Toulouse. Labor Day this year is also the first since the establishment of the Unified General Confederation of Labor. The main leaders of the Unified General Confederation of Labor have issued a notice to all affiliated labor unions, urging them to hold many gatherings to celebrate the occasion. All cadres of labor unions and their members should participate and list the demands put forward by the working class, the most important of which are as follows: Implement a 40-hour work week; Laborers can sign collective contracts with employers; Implement the program of building public works proposed by the former General Confederation of Labor to relieve unemployment. It is generally believed that only private industries, the construction industry, and traveling car drivers will stop work on this day, while public utilities will continue to work as usual. (Havas dispatch, 30th)

Edinburgh University Students Kidnap a Female Performer for Charity 31

Broadway stage actress and famous female comedy writer, Herston, was forcibly taken away in a car by fifteen Edinburgh University students at the Empire Theatre. At the time, the woman was only wearing tight-fitting clothes. The students demanded a ransom of thirty-five pounds to help charitable causes. Now all fifteen people have admitted to the crime, and the principal, Holland, has notified the woman's husband, Ahearn, and said that he has revoked the special university privileges of the offending students. The manager of the Empire Theatre and the owner of the troupe have applied for leniency on behalf of the students. Although the woman injured her ankle and suffered several abrasions when she was kidnapped, she also joined the ranks of those seeking leniency. However, the police authorities attach great importance to this matter and plan to prosecute the students involved. (Reuters dispatch, 30th)

Britain Expands its Navy; 38 Ships to be Built This Year; Naval Budget Increased by 10 Million Pounds; Equipment at Singapore Naval Base Further Supplemented 32

(London) The Admiralty will issue a white paper today explaining the navy's plan to implement the new defense proposals this year, and will announce an additional budget of about 10 million pounds. This amount will be added to the additional 10 million pounds already announced for the air force. (Reuters dispatch, 30th)

(London) It was announced today that the supplementary naval budget for the current fiscal year is 10 million pounds. According to the 1936 plan, the navy will add 38 warships in addition to small warships. This budget is based on the defense policy explained in the white paper of March 3. The various warships to be built are as follows: 2 battleships, 5 cruisers, 9 destroyers, 1 aircraft carrier, 4 submarines (1 mine-laying submarine, 1 patrol submarine, 2 small submarines), 6 gunboats, 1 river gunboat, 2 special service ships, 6 motor torpedo boats, and other small warships. The supplementary budget also stipulates important improvement expenses for storing munitions, fuel, and other important military supplies. The needs of new air force equipment, such as new types of aircraft, are also stipulated. It is reported that the authorities have decided to install anti-aircraft guns on each ship as soon as possible. The funds for this purpose are also included in the supplementary budget for this session, and will continue to be handled in this way in the future. The four Hawkins-class cruisers currently equipped with 7.5-inch guns, which were listed as 8-inch gun cruisers under the 1930 London Naval Treaty, were originally scheduled to be dismantled by the end of this year, but it has now been decided to preserve them, and three of them will be converted to 6.1-inch guns and included in the B-class tonnage cruisers. One ship will be converted into an officer training ship and will not be used for war. The old aircraft carrier Argus has been converted into a training ship. All these changes have been notified to the signatories of the London Naval Treaty. The needs of the Singapore naval base have been carefully considered and it is believed that it should be further supplemented, so the expenditure has been increased from 8,693,000 pounds to 10,661,000 pounds. Dry docks capable of accommodating the largest ships will be built in Plymouth and Gibraltar. (Reuters dispatch, 30th)

US Presidential Election; Results of Primary Elections in Massachusetts and Pennsylvania; Roosevelt's Candidacy More Assured 34

(Washington) President Roosevelt's hope of being nominated as the Democratic presidential candidate is more assured today as a result of the primary elections in Massachusetts and Pennsylvania yesterday. As for the most noteworthy development in the political world, it is that the Republican Party has apparently begun to campaign to obstruct the power of Kansas Governor Landon. The results of yesterday's primary elections in the two states can increase the political disputes, but cannot indicate the direction of the Republican Party. The president and Landon both won victories in Massachusetts, but this cannot be regarded as a formal competition because the names of the candidates were not written on the ballot, and the voters had to write them themselves. Only Landon was campaigning in the state. The Republican Party in the state cast a total of 94,953 votes, Landon received 78,259 votes, former President Hoover received 7,812 votes, and Chicago publisher Knox received 2,102 votes. For the Democratic Party, President Roosevelt received 31,459 votes, Smith received 1,443 votes, and Father Coughlin received 993 votes. In Pennsylvania, a lawyer from New York, Blagden, received the support of conservatives and competed with President Roosevelt. Reports from about 5,000 of the 7,962 electoral districts in the state show that Roosevelt received 393,062 votes, and Blagden received only 23,472 votes. For the Republican Party, it was only Senator Borah, and there was no competition, and he received a total of 254,613 votes. However, the Republican Party in both states is not bound and can still elect others in the future, unlike the Democratic Party, which must elect President Roosevelt. (National Telegram, 29th)

Giving Equal Importance to Continental Policy; Japan Seeks to Establish Maritime Policy; Strengthen Administrative Organs in the South Seas and Taiwan; Seek Overseas Development to Solve Overpopulation 37

(Tokyo) The Japanese government intends to ensure Japan's position as a force for stability in East Asia in order to actively promote world peace and human culture. It has abandoned the naval reduction treaty and abolished the principle of the open door. The Japanese Navy believes that in order to ensure Japan's future survival and realize the essence of being a force for stability in East Asia, the adjustment of the continental policy aimed at developing Manchuria and the maritime national policy with the highest goal of peace in the Pacific is an urgent task. Therefore, in the future, the three ministries of the army, navy, and foreign affairs plan to link the continental policy and the maritime policy together to establish a national policy as the foundation of Japan's domestic and foreign policies. The reason for establishing the maritime policy as an urgent task is that Japan has a narrow territory and a lack of natural resources, but its population is overpopulated and its growth rate is increasing. To solve this population problem, there is no other way than to transfer population, develop resources, and open up markets overseas. Therefore, the Ministry of the Navy, on the one hand, strengthens national defense and promotes the national spirit of overseas development. On the other hand, it pays attention to foreign countries and maintains diplomatic relations with countries surrounding the Pacific Ocean, adjusting conflicts of interest in commerce and trade. At the same time, it strengthens the administrative organs in the South Seas and Taiwan, supports commerce and trade, and develops maritime transport and fisheries in order to achieve the goal of overseas population transfer. (Domei News Agency dispatch, 30th)

India and Australia successively boycott Japanese silk. Japanese goods' attempts to develop in South America also fail. Japan prepares to boycott Australian wool and wheat. 44

(Tokyo) The Japan Silk Manufacturers Association received a telegram from Bombay stating that the Indian Parliament would soon pass a bill to greatly increase the import tax on Japanese silk. It is said that the bill will stipulate that in addition to the current tariff of 25%, a special tax of 14 annas per pound will be added. In other words, the tax required for Japanese silk to be transported to India, calculated at the current value, will be no less than 567%. Such a heavy tax is tantamount to prohibiting the import of Japanese silk. The purpose of this bill is to protect the silk industry of Kashmir and Bengal. However, Japanese merchants say that Japanese silk does not compete with Indian silk because their uses are different. The Indian government's move to increase taxes is merely to use this as a tool for negotiating the expiring Indo-Japanese cotton trade agreement, and to give special preferential treatment to British silk imported into India. It is reported that in the year from April 1935 to March 1936, India imported 3 million pounds of silk from various countries, worth 7.8 million rupees, of which Japanese silk accounted for half, while British silk was only 500,000 pounds, worth 1 million rupees. (30th Reuters)

(Tokyo) The Japanese Commercial Survey Mission went to various countries in Central and South America last autumn, hoping to adjust Japan's commercial relations, but ultimately failed. Colombia has concluded a trade agreement with the United States and cannot accept Japan's early negotiations. Negotiations with Ecuador on the purchase of industrial salt were almost completed, but were still abandoned when officially signing the agreement. Oil purchase negotiations with Venezuela could not proceed due to the death of President Gómez and the instability of the political situation. As for coffee and coconuts produced in Santo Domingo, the Japanese hoped that trade with Japan would increase, but the movement to negotiate a commercial treaty was ultimately unsuccessful, and the Santo Domingo government even intended to increase import duties on Japanese goods. Imports of Japanese goods into Haiti are subject to a 100% ad valorem tax. The Haitian government claims that if Japan purchases cotton produced by Haiti worth 70 to 80 million yen annually, the import duty can be reduced appropriately. However, in reality, Japan cannot purchase cotton worth 70 to 80 million yen from Haiti every year. Among the above-mentioned countries that have a commercial treaty with Japan, Ecuador's treaty will also expire on May 15. Therefore, Japan's commercial relations with South America may ultimately not be able to make progress. (30th Reuters)

(Tokyo) The Japanese business community expects the Tariff Investigation Committee to hold an extraordinary meeting tomorrow, advocating a 12% ad valorem tax on wool imported from Australia. The committee will invoke the Trade Protection Law to consider boycotting Australian wool and wheat, in retaliation for Australia's recent increase in import duties on Japanese cotton cloth and rayon. It is reported that in 1935, the goods imported by Japan from Australia were mostly raw wool, totaling 35 million yuan, while the goods exported by Japan to Australia totaled 75 million yuan. (30th Reuters)

Chairman Chiang instructs students of various schools in Jiangxi. Xiong Shihui and Miao Peicheng pay respects and report on the political situation. Meets with Yang Xiaobo and others, inquiring about Jiangxi's finances. 45

(Nanchang) Chairman Chiang, accompanied by Qian Dajun and Xiong Shihui, went to Xishan by car at 3 pm on the 30th to instruct high school students from various schools. He returned to the Nanchang branch of the Lixing Society at 6 pm, met with Miao Peicheng, who reported on the duties of the Inspectorate. He then met with Yang Xiaobo, manager of the Nanchang Central Bank, and Chen Wei, manager of the Jiangxi Yumin Bank, who reported on the bank's affairs and the recent financial situation in Jiangxi. At 7 pm, Chairman Chiang went to Beitan Park for a walk, and then returned to the Lixing Society for dinner. (30th Central News Agency)

(Nanchang) Chairman Chiang instructed the military training students of various high schools in Jiangxi at Xishan on the afternoon of the 30th. Xiong Shihui, Qian Dajun, and more than 800 students stood respectfully to listen to the instructions for an hour. The main points of the instructions are as follows: The purpose of your training here is to save the country. All academic research, physical exercise, and spiritual and moral cultivation, etc., should all strive towards this goal. Not only should you make such purposeful efforts during military training, but you must also recognize the meaning of our lives and the purpose of our lives, so as to establish a revolutionary outlook on life. No matter when, where, or what, you should adhere to a firm belief, a correct direction, and an honest attitude, and follow the path of righteousness and brightness, and move forward bravely. You must not be confused, perfunctory, or procrastinate for a moment or a matter. You must know that the psychology and habits of perfunctory confusion are the root of self-destruction and national subjugation. We must fundamentally eradicate them, and then we can improve our virtue day by day and become glorious modern citizens. The content of so-called "military training," the study of all military academic subjects, is only a necessary part. Its most important task is the training of military spirit and the cultivation of personality. We should know that soldiers are the citizens with the highest personality, the strongest spirit, the most diligent life, the most ambitious aspirations, the most able to sacrifice for the country, and the most honorable and noble. The purpose of military training now is to cultivate this kind of truly militarized youth to be a model for the people and a vanguard for saving the country. How can a true military spirit and personality be cultivated? The primary condition is to strictly abide by discipline. This so-called "discipline" not only refers to all laws and military discipline, nor is it limited to a certain time and place for attending classes and drills. Its correct meaning is that our every move, every word, and every action should conform to the principles of etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame, and follow a certain reasonable standard, no matter when, where, or what. In short, it is the strict regularization of our entire lives, which is true militarization. If we want to truly abide by discipline, so as to cultivate the highest personality and the strongest spirit of a true soldier, we must develop the ability to be autonomous and self-governing, and work hard to be cautious and sincere. We must first eradicate the evil thoughts of selfishness and self-interest, and establish the great ambition of saving the country and the people, so that our hearts are as bright as the blue sky and the white sun, and we have no shame in what we do, and everything can be told to others. Only in this way can we cultivate the spirit and personality of a soldier who stands upright between heaven and earth, and then we can be good citizens and strong soldiers of the country, and then we can accomplish the great cause of saving the country and reviving the nation. You students should encourage each other. (30th Central News Agency)

The League of Nations Administrative Council. Our country wins a council seat. Expected to attend the meeting in September. 47

(Geneva) After the Organizational Committee of the League of Nations Administrative Council closed last night, a reporter from the Central News Agency interviewed Ambassador Guo Taiqi. According to his conversation, the representatives of the committee all felt that China's request to rejoin the Administrative Council was extremely reasonable and could prove that although the League of Nations is now in a precarious situation, China's belief in the League of Nations has not diminished. The current situation of the League of Nations is indeed extremely pessimistic. Not only has its international prestige declined, but its future fate is also unknown. However, if Asian countries are excluded from the Administrative Council for a long time, it will be detrimental to both the universality and consolidation of the League of Nations. Ambassador Guo finally said that he believes that the Administrative Council will accept the report of the Organizational Committee, and China is expected to rejoin the Administrative Council in September. (29th Central News Agency)

(Geneva) The committee on the distribution of council member seats of the League of Nations Administrative Council has been meeting for days to discuss China's request for a council seat. A result has been reached. A public announcement has been issued by the Secretariat of the League of Nations, which reads, "The committee has decided to recommend to the Administrative Council that the number of non-permanent council seats be temporarily increased from nine to eleven until September 1939 (Note: The Administrative Council originally had five permanent council seats, namely the five countries of Britain, France, Germany, Italy, and Japan. Now Germany and Japan have withdrawn from the League, and the Soviet Union has been newly added, totaling four seats.) One of the two newly added seats is the one added in 1933 and currently occupied by Portugal, which should still be maintained. In the future, it will be granted to member countries outside of Europe that do not belong to any group (the so-called groups refer to the Scandinavian Peninsula, the Little Entente, Latin America, etc.). The second seat will be granted to countries on the Asian continent. In the committee's opinion, it can be granted to China. As for the term of the newly added council seats, some national representatives in the committee advocated a term of one year, so that the Administrative Council and the League of Nations General Assembly can have room for flexibility when the Administrative Council is engaged in a general reform in a short period of time. Other national representatives advocated a term of three years, which is the same as the usual term of non-permanent council members. However, during these three years, the Administrative Council can still be unrestricted if it is engaged in reorganization. As a result, the committee passed the second method with nine votes for, five votes against, and two abstentions." (29th Havas)

Guangdong Province: Actively Developing the Sugar Industry; The Entire Province Divided into Five Sugarcane Cultivation Zones; Total Capital Reaches Over Nine Million Yuan 61

Guangzhou Correspondence: In light of the fact that China's sugar industry has been increasingly heading towards bankruptcy due to the dumping of foreign sugar and the impact of the global economic crisis, the Guangdong provincial authorities, recognizing that Guangdong Province has always been a major sugar-producing region in China and that the province should make the greatest efforts to revive the sugar industry, have designated sugar industry development as one of the important tasks in the first three-year administrative plan. After three years of implementation, the results have been quite considerable. It is noted that the three-year plan for sugar industry development involves first dividing the province into five sugarcane cultivation zones in areas suitable for sugarcane cultivation: Guangzhou Zone (Panyu, Dongguan, Shunde, Nanhai, and the Pearl River Delta); Huizhou-Yangjiang Zone (Huiyang, Boluo, Haifeng, Lufeng); Chaozhou-Shantou Zone (Chaoyang, Jieyang, Huilai, Puning); Xuwen Zone (Xuwen, Haikang); and Qiongya Zone (all counties under Qiongya). The first areas to be prepared and established are the Guangzhou, Huizhou-Yangjiang, and Chaozhou-Shantou zones. The current status of each of these zones is recorded below:

Guangzhou Zone: Sugarcane factories have been established in Xinzhao and Shitou, Panyu, respectively. Also, one factory each has been established in Shunde and Dongguan. (One factory each has been established in the Huizhou-Yangjiang and Chaozhou-Shantou zones.) The total cost of startup and temporary annual expenses reaches over 9,402,000 yuan. The Xinzhao sugar factory covers an area of 110 mu, and the cost of machinery and factory construction is estimated at 1,474,056 yuan. The Xinzhao factory is also equipped with an alcohol factory. The Shitou factory covers an area of 175 mu, and the cost of machinery and factory construction is estimated at 4,035,320 yuan. The Xinzhao and Shitou factories can each press 1,500 tons of sugarcane per day, equivalent to 16.8 dan per ton, for a total of approximately 25,200 dan of sugarcane pressed, producing 180 tons of sugar, equivalent to approximately 3,024 dan. The Shunde factory is located in Xiachun Village, opposite Rongqi in the county, covering an area of 250 mu. The construction cost is 376,200 Hong Kong dollars. The full set of sugarcane pressing machinery costs 140,000 British pounds. This machine can press 1,000 tons of sugarcane daily, producing over 100 tons of clean Java No. 24 white sugar. The construction cost of the Dongguan factory is 450,000 Hong Kong dollars. The entire set of machinery costs 140,000 British pounds, with an additional 1,700 British pounds for chemical laboratory instruments and light railways.

Huizhou-Yangjiang Zone: The construction site is located at Pingtan, 80 li from Huiyang, as the factory site. The cost of machinery factories and a 5,000-ton warehouse, including a full set of sugarcane pressing machinery, totals 700,000 US dollars, with an additional 27,921 US dollars for accessories. The alcohol machinery costs 194,229 Hong Kong dollars, with an additional 10,140 yuan for accessories. The Izatte machine costs 43,377 Hong Kong dollars. This factory can press 1,000 tons of sugarcane per day, equivalent to 16,800 dan, producing 100 tons of sugar, equivalent to 1,680 dan?

Chaozhou-Shantou Zone: The first sugarcane cultivation site is located in Guitou Village, Quxi, Jieyang, covering an area of over 120 mu. The cost of machinery and construction totals 552,000 US dollars. The factory can press 750 tons of sugarcane per day.

Xuwen Zone and Qiongya Zone: Still in the planning and preparation stages. Statistics on the sugar products produced in each zone include Grade A white sugar, Grade B white sugar, No. 1 coarse sugar, No. 2 coarse sugar, fire sugar, sugar frost, and cube sugar. The quality is better than that of imported products. In terms of sales and distribution, the provincial government has established a provincial product management office, dividing the province into eight operating zones. In Shanghai, there is also a Guangdong product management branch responsible for promoting Guangdong sugar to other provinces. Business is quite developed. In terms of personnel, each factory has hired foreign engineers from Honolulu, USA, and the Czech Republic to be responsible for the factory, and there are also mechanical and engineering students who have graduated from abroad and returned to assist in factory affairs. In addition, there are over 100 high school graduates interning at the factory. The Military Reclamation Office has also established a sugar industry personnel training institute at the Pingtan factory. After graduation, they will all serve in the factory. Once the engineering is proficient, each factory will no longer need to hire foreigners.

Regarding the issue of raw material sugarcane, personnel have been sent to the Philippines to collect 52 kinds of excellent sugarcane varieties from that area. Several excellent sugarcane seedling propagation sites have been established throughout the province: Xinzhou Propagation Site, covering an area of 450 mu; Misha Propagation Site, covering an area of 120 mu; Chencun Propagation Site, covering an area of 400 mu; and Agricultural and Forestry Bureau Propagation Site, covering an area of 500 mu. The Huiyang factory has two sugarcane seedling sites, covering a total of 100 mu. Recently, it is planned to add another one, covering an area of 700 mu. In total, the propagation sites cover a total of 2,000 mu. The area operated by private individuals is not yet included. In total, there are approximately 8,000 mu of public and private newly planted sugarcane seedling propagation sites in the province, which is sufficient for 130,000 mu of sugarcane fields. These excellent sugarcane varieties can yield an average of 120 dan of sugarcane per mu, and 10 dan can produce 140 jin of sugar. Each mu of sugarcane can produce 15-16 dan of sugar. The program is still being actively promoted, and farmers are being assisted in propagation. According to this plan, if implemented step by step, the revival and development of Guangdong's sugar industry is inevitable, and the widespread planting of sugarcane fields by farmers will have a significant impact on the rural economy. Currently, the Guangdong authorities are conducting a detailed assessment of the achievements of the first three-year plan and preparing to formulate a second three-year plan for sugar industry development in order to achieve further success.

Guangdong Construction Department Stipulates: Private Enterprise Plans; Promoting the Realization of the Three-Year Plan; Guiding the People to Directly Run Real Industries; Assigning Subordinates to Draft Detailed Plans 62

Guangzhou Correspondence: He Qili, Director of the Guangdong Provincial Construction Department, believes that as the second three-year plan for Guangdong Province is about to begin implementation, in order to plan for the program, the government should do its best to promote it on the construction side, and it is also extremely important to guide the people to directly manage it so as to achieve twice the result with half the effort. Therefore, he specifically ordered the Bureau of Agriculture and Forestry, the Bureau of Port Affairs, the Industrial Testing Institute, the Provincial Long-Distance Telephone Management Committee, and the fifth section of the department, as well as technician Yu Ji, to draft private enterprise plans as a standard for compiling the second three-year plan. The original order stated, "Our country's science is backward, and the production industry is far inferior to others. The outflow of money every year is truly alarming. Even agriculture, which is said to be the foundation of our country, is stuck in the old ways of production methods, and the output is not abundant, and a large amount needs to be imported. Not to mention the others. In addition, in recent years, countries around the world have been affected by the recession, and each has adopted a policy of dumping at low prices, using our country as the end of their surplus products. As a result, the collapse of our country's rural areas and the decline of industry and commerce are increasing day by day. In this situation, how can the national economy and the people's livelihood not decline day by day? The provincial government has taken this into account and has formulated a three-year administrative plan, with particular emphasis on the path of real industry construction. During these three years, the scale has been roughly established, and those that are relatively complicated and have not yet been completed are also proceeding step by step to achieve success as scheduled. Among them, the scale is relatively large and inconvenient for private operation, so the government first organizes them to show its promotion. However, in recent years, private real industries have not seen any progress. The reason is that most businessmen lack technical knowledge, so they are not willing to try easily. In order to revive the agricultural, forestry, and sericulture industries in the five provinces and develop various new industries, the department should proceed with what should be done on the government side, and especially guide the people to directly run it, so as to achieve twice the result with half the effort. Therefore, the department has determined the items of various construction projects and designated personnel to be responsible for drafting construction plans separately, so that if the people want to run any industry, they can use this as a bridge. The items and responsible personnel are listed as follows: Forestry, fishery, and water conservancy are the responsibility of the Bureau of Agriculture and Forestry; shipping is the responsibility of the Bureau of Port Affairs; sericulture and weaving and dyeing are the responsibility of the Sericulture Improvement Bureau; chemical industry and leather manufacturing are the responsibility of the Industrial Testing Institute; the electrical industry is the responsibility of the Provincial Long-Distance Telephone Management Committee; the mining industry is the responsibility of the fifth section of the department; and agricultural tool manufacturing, oil pressing, and stationery manufacturing are the responsibility of Yu Ji, a technician of the department. Among the above plans, the required items must be thoroughly investigated to ensure that they are practical, so that the people can see them and put them into practice without any hindrance, and within the possible scope, the size of their scale should be distinguished separately, and two plans should be drafted for the same industry, so that those who intend to run it but have less capital can also benefit from it. The above-mentioned designated personnel must follow this purpose and draft and submit detailed plans within two months of receiving the document for review and publication. In addition to separate orders, this order is hereby issued to order you to comply immediately, this order."

Zhejiang and Jiangxi Provinces: Specialty Products Exhibition Begins; A Total of Eleven Departments of Exhibits; More Than 10,000 Kinds of Local Specialties 63

Hangzhou Correspondence: In order to promote economic cooperation, the authorities of Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces have initiated a joint exhibition of specialty products. The Zhejiang Provincial Bureau of Commerce and Administration drafted a plan, which was submitted to the Zhejiang Provincial Government for approval and obtained the consent of the Jiangxi Provincial Government and the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Council. The first preparatory meeting was held in Yushan, and the charter of the conference, the opening date, the cost sharing, and the free transportation were approved. Later, the Zhejiang Provincial Association for the Promotion of National Products initiated a national products exhibition. Because the aims were the same, they joined and merged the organization. A preparatory office was established, and committees, sponsors, and staff were appointed to begin handling manufacturer registration and soliciting exhibits. The National Products Exhibition Hall on Yingzi Road and the buildings of the Bureau of Commerce and Administration were selected as venues. After active preparation and arrangement, everything is ready.

Exhibits: The exhibits include all the products of the counties in Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces, as well as other national products. There are a total of more than 10,000 kinds. The exhibition hall is divided into eleven departments, with a total of forty-five rooms. The first department displays embroidery and silk fabrics. The second department displays new and old medicines, educational supplies, and paper. The third department displays ham, dried white fish, lotus root flour, water shield, and other foods. The fourth department displays cosmetics, artworks, scissors, fans, condensed milk, etc. The fifth department displays copper, tin, porcelain, swords, rattan and bamboo ware, and food and beverages. The sixth department displays silks and satins from various counties. The seventh department displays specimens from the Entomology Bureau and local products along the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway. The eighth and ninth departments are entirely for the display of national products. The tenth department displays agricultural products, minerals, aquatic products, and models of the Qiantang River Bridge. The eleventh department displays silk, cocoons, and satin produced in Hangzhou. All the items are extremely precious, such as Du Jinsheng's silk fabrics, the paper from Yuhang, Jiangshan, and Quzhou counties, the ham from Dongyang, the dried fish from Yongjia, the tea from Longjing and Tianmu, the scissors from Zhang Xiaoquan, the face powder from Kong Fengchun, the fans from Shu Lianji, the Longquan swords, the Jianhu yellow wine, the Huzhou zongzi, the Hangzhou silk and satin, and other agricultural products, which are provided by the Provincial Rice and Wheat Farm and the Cotton Farm, and minerals and aquatic products, which are sent by the Mineral Resources Survey Institute and the Aquatic Products Testing Ground for display. All the products of Zhejiang can be seen at a glance, and the production capacity can also be inspected once, which is quite meaningful compared with other national products exhibitions.

Opening Ceremony: The conference venue is decorated quite luxuriously. The opening time is 2:00 p.m. on May 1st. Wu Tingyang, Director of the Construction Department, serves as the chairman of the conference. Huang Shaohong, Chairman of the Provincial Government, also attended and gave a speech. At the same time, the conference invited famous party and government figures in the province to take turns giving speeches on the significance of the specialty products exhibition on the provincial radio station. (April 30th)

Anhui Tea Export Registration; Preparing to Control Wholesale in the Province; Seven Registration Locations Set Up 64

Wuhu Correspondence: During the tea sales season in Anhui Province last year, the Finance and Construction Departments jointly established tea export registration offices in the border areas to clarify the sales situation in preparation for improving tea. As a result, a portion of Qihong tea this year was able to be preliminarily loaned based on the registered quantity last year, and the government supervised the sales. Now, new tea is pouring out and is starting to proceed. Considering that tea is the largest agricultural product in Anhui Province and is mostly sold abroad, its prosperity and decline are not only related to the rural economy of Anhui Province but also to China's foreign trade. Last year, due to various obstacles in the mainland due to weather and human affairs, the output was not strong. Although the registration system was established, the actual sales situation was still not fully understood. This year, the two departments will first supervise and sell Qimen black tea. If the trial is effective, next year they will further plan and proceed in the entire Anhui tea area. Recently, after the Qingming Festival, tea has been launched on the market, and the time for sales and export has arrived. The establishment of the registration office is more important than last year, and it cannot be delayed. However, due to the changes in Qihong and local transportation, the location and organization of the office should be slightly changed compared to last year. This year's tea business tax has already been set up and levied, and the establishment of various registration offices at the same time will also be beneficial to the inspection of tax revenue. The registration office organization location and the expenses to be paid have been made into a table, and registration methods and notification formats have been drafted and submitted to the provincial government's 538th standing meeting for approval and implementation. The directors of the respective offices have been appointed to start operations separately. Herewith, the registration methods are attached and ordered to Wuhu. Datong. The two public security bureaus and the Xuanzhou. Hefei. Huaiyuan. And other county governments, first jointly with the directors of the registration offices, record and announce to the tea merchants to fill out the application form when reporting taxes, and report to the registration office when transporting them for export. At the same time, they are divided into various departments to carefully maintain them. The registration locations are Wuhu. Xuanzhou. Street entrance. Daohu. Datong. Huaiyuan. Sanhe and other seven locations. The expenses for six months are estimated at 10,200 yuan. (April 29th)

Anyang Excavation Team Unearths Site of Yin Dynasty Architecture; Also Unearths Skeletal Remains of Ancient Race 65

Anyang Correspondence: The Anyang Yin Ruins Excavation Team of the Institute of History and Language of the Academia Sinica has been collecting since 1928. Until last winter, there were twelve collections. This spring is the thirteenth collection of excavations, which will be hosted by Guo Ziheng, Li Chunyi, Gao Xiaomei, Wang Zixiang, Yin Ziwen, Pan Shijun, and Shi Zhangru, seven staff members sent by the institute, and Sun Wenqing from the Henan Museum sent by the Henan Provincial Government will participate in the excavation. Work began on March 19th and is scheduled to be completed by the end of June. However, depending on the work situation, the time may be extended. Initially, only 60 to 70 workers were used, but now, due to the large area, there are already 100 workers. In the future, the number of workers required for the work will increase even more. The address is located in the northeast of Xiaotun Village, west of Anyang City, on the west bank of the Binhe River, which is high and has sticky soil. Since the start of work, the excavation area is 7 to 8 mu. The purpose is to clarify the entire architectural map of the Yin Ruins. If gray pits and tomb passages are encountered, they will also be excavated incidentally, so the unearthed items are less than the previous collections. The pottery, shells, bones, and stones that have been excavated so far are not particularly unique. In the excavated area, in addition to the mixed and messy gray pits and Tang Dynasty tomb passages, a small part of the Yin Dynasty palace foundation and cemetery have been exposed. The two places are more than a hundred steps apart. The cemetery is in the south. Six tomb pits have now been excavated, arranged in east-west rows, in two rows. Each pit is full of white bones, lying face up, lying face down, squeezed into the pit, about six or seven people. Judging from the situation, this cemetery is a mass burial pit from the Yin Dynasty or after the Yin Dynasty. The skeletons in the pit are all intact, and they are thought to be buried with the emperor after his death, or they were prisoners of war or rebels who were executed and buried there. After the skeletons are taken out, the anthropology team of the institute will measure their skulls to study the evolution and development of human brains in history. Many stone blocks of column bases and ancient wall engineering have been exposed at the palace site. The wall foundations are arranged vertically and horizontally in rows, with varying widths and narrowness, all of which are remnants of the main hall and side rooms. Many of the wall or column bases have been destroyed by the tomb passages of the Tang Dynasty. The construction of Tang Dynasty tombs was different from that of modern times. The tomb passages were dug from the ground, the coffins were placed in the cave, and the tombs were sealed, so the walls of the Yin Ruins were destroyed a lot. In addition to each person taking care of a pit during the excavation, the staff of the team spends most of their time organizing, washing, numbering, and packing the antiques. They get up at 5:00 every morning, and the work is extremely intense. (April 27th)

Changshu: Collapse of Cloth Factory House; Casualties 68

The Yufeng Cloth Factory in Xiao Jialangxia, Da Dongdou, suddenly collapsed on the afternoon of the 29th. Some of the houses suddenly collapsed, and the female workers in the spinning room were unable to escape in time, resulting in many people being crushed inside. As a result, an old woman, who was 63 years old, died on the spot. Her head was broken and her feet were broken, and her condition was extremely tragic. There were also six people who were seriously injured. As for the cause of the disaster, the factory houses were originally old-fashioned houses that were rebuilt. They had been in disrepair for a long time, causing the main beam to break, creating this tragedy. After the accident, according to Wang Dingrong, the manager of the factory, Wang Gu, the deceased old woman, was compensated 150 yuan, and she was buried immediately. The six injured female workers were sent to the Jishan Hospital in Beimen for treatment. At present, all work in the factory has been suspended, and work can only resume after the factory building is repaired.

Suzhou: Trial of Labor-Management Lawsuit at Yarn Factory 69

The Su Lun Yarn Factory outside Panmen, due to a conflict between female worker Jiang Fengying and Zhu Yindi, involved the factory director and the director of factory affairs, resulting in mutual accusations of defamation, obstruction of freedom, and damage. Yesterday (30th) was the date for the public trial by the local court. The court tried the two cases of Jiang Fengying accusing Zhu Yindi of obstructing freedom and Zhu Yindi accusing Jiang Fengying of obstructing freedom and damage. Zhu Yindi, accompanied by her mother Zhu Jiang, and defense lawyer Huang Jue, and Jiang Fengying, accompanied by her mother Jiang Zhu, and defense lawyers Liu Zuwang and Liu Zuyin, reported one after another. At 10:00 a.m., female judge Chen Ziguan opened the court for trial. According to Jiang Fengying, Zhu Yindi and her mother scolded her for being the concubine of the four young masters (i.e., factory director Yan Xinqi) and Pu Liangyuan (i.e., director of factory affairs), and demanded that they publish an apology in the newspaper for one month and compensate for the loss of reputation of one yuan. Zhu Yindi also stated that Jiang Fengying asked her to marry Pu Liangyuan, and she refused, holding a grudge. She ganged up with her mother Jiang Zhu and other eight people to rush to her home and smash tables, benches, bowls, and other items, demanding that they publish an apology in the newspaper for seven days and compensate for the damaged items. After a debate between the two sides, it was decided to announce the verdict on May 7th. Zhu Yindi and her mother were released on bail, and the rest were ordered to return. As for the two cases of Yan Xinqi and Pu Liangyuan separately accusing Zhu Yindi of defamation, there is no date for the hearing yet. The society has paid a lot of attention to this case, so the gallery was extremely crowded when the court opened yesterday.

Wuxi: County Government Security Team Makes Earnest Contact 70

The Wuxi District Administrative Inspector and District Security Commander believes that although the county government and the security brigade have different institutions and responsibilities, local administration and local military affairs should originally be in contact to cooperate with each other. However, since the county magistrate no longer concurrently served as the brigade commander, the organizational system is not connected, and the powers are not concentrated. He is deeply afraid that the contact will be lost over time, reducing administrative efficiency. Yesterday, he specially telegraphed the counties under his jurisdiction and the security brigade commander that they should make earnest contact with each other on county administration and security team affairs in the future to achieve the effect of mutual assistance. He also stipulated four measures to achieve consistency. The measures are as follows: Although the team affairs of each county are routine and minor, if any contact occurs, it must be handled in writing; the county government and security team should report to the district command for approval to add or transfer security squadron platoons; if the brigade headquarters is stationed in County A and the squadron platoon is stationed in County B, if it is necessary to transfer them, it should consult with the County B government and obtain its consent, and report to the district for approval before implementation; the headquarters will simultaneously order the relevant county governments to investigate the dispatch matters of the security teams under its jurisdiction.

Spring Silkworms Collected in Four Villages 71

Recently, the weather has turned better, and the rainfall has been even, and the mulberry leaves have developed luxuriantly. Spring sericulture is progressing step by step and has reached the common breeding period. At present, most of the early-stage spring silkworms in each village have been collected in the past two days. The silkworms are in very good condition. The remaining late-stage spring silkworms must also be collected uniformly within the next week. The staff of the model sericulture zone, the central guidance office in each district, and the sub-guidance office in this county have been busy with guidance work in recent days. The output this year will definitely increase by more than 30% compared to previous years, so the future market price of mulberry leaves will definitely be expensive. At present, the leaf price in the southern village has reached about 2 yuan per dan.

Zhong Jihe, the captain of the detective team of the County Public Security Bureau, received a secret report the day before yesterday, saying that there was a bandit chief named Wang Tingfu (i.e., Qian Hegen) who had committed many crimes and was now hiding under Huinong Bridge. Please send a team to arrest him quickly. After receiving the report, Captain Zhong immediately sent detective Dai Qian, along with detectives Zhang Xiaodi and others, to arrest him, as the bandit had been wanted twice before. Changzhou: Conference on Properties and Assets of Eight Counties Under Old Prefecture 73

鑫誠奎 Lumberyard Robbed 74

The Xinchengkui Lumberyard, located along the Nanhe River outside the West Gate of Wuyi, is owned by Yu Mairu from Anhui. His family lives to the south of the lumberyard. At approximately 2:00 AM on the 29th, seven or eight bandits suddenly entered the premises, each carrying box guns and flashlights. They searched and looted the place, first going to the bedroom of Yu Mairu's niece, but found nothing. They then went to Mairu's bedroom and demanded silence, robbing him of 105 silver dollars, gold and silver jewelry, clothing, and other items, estimated to be worth several hundred dollars. Yu's niece seized the opportunity to hide in the lumberyard and report the crime. The lumberyard workers immediately armed themselves and went to the roof. Realizing the danger, the robbers fled with their loot. Afterwards, the local Public Security First Sub-station reported the incident to the Public Security Bureau, requesting police assistance in the pursuit. At dawn, employee Cui Yulin and others chased a man to the vicinity of Dongdai Town, where he fled into the river to hide. They captured him and took him to the station, where he confessed to the robbery and implicated several accomplices. The police are currently intensifying their search.

Danyang: Farmland in Huangling Township Flooded 75

Jiang Rou’er and others from Xihu Village in Hubin Township, Zhenjiang County, built a dam to divert the flow of the Central River, obstructing the irrigation of Huangling and other townships in this county, causing disputes. Zhu Changfa and others from Huangling Township had submitted a petition to the district office, requesting it to be forwarded to the Provincial Construction Department to order the Zhenjiang County government to demolish the dam. Unexpectedly, the weather has been overcast and rainy in recent days, with thunderstorms and flash floods. The water level in the Central River has risen sharply. Due to the earthen dam built by Jiang Kao’er and others from Xihu Village in Zhenjiang County, the water flow could not be discharged, causing it to overflow onto the banks. This has resulted in the flooding of over a thousand acres of farmland on both sides of the river in Huling, Xihu Village, and Malinghou Maling Village in this county. Currently, the township head and the flooded landowners are submitting a petition to the county government requesting relief.

Zhenjiang: Fire Kills 76

The Hongshengxiang Cigarette and Paper Shop on Boxian Road in Zhenjiang caught fire at approximately 9:00 PM last night (the 29th) due to careless electrical wiring. The fire spread to the neighboring Mingji Laundry and the Xinchang Clock Repair Shop. When the fire broke out, Zhang Yanqing, the owner of Hongshengxiang, rushed upstairs to salvage items and was surrounded by flames, unable to escape. He was later rescued, but his head was burned, and his body was severely charred. He was immediately taken to the hospital for treatment, where his life is in critical danger. At the same time, Chen Qishan and his wife, the owners of Mingji Laundry, were playing nearby when the fire started. Only their five-year-old daughter was sleeping upstairs. Due to the lack of time for rescue, the child was burned to death on the spot. After firefighters from various fire brigades fought to extinguish the blaze, it was finally put out at approximately 10:00 PM.

Nantong: Giant Snake Discovered in Beijige Pavilion 77

The Beijige Pavilion in Tongcheng is built on the north gate of Bizhai, a remote location rarely visited by people. Recently, the ring road around the city was constructed, and the number of visitors has gradually increased. The abbot, Monk Xintian, was demolishing a hole in the city wall because people were climbing onto the pavilion. On the morning of the 28th, while cutting through the thorns to block the hole, a snake's head as large as a fist suddenly emerged from the wall hole and exhaled at the monk before retracting. The monk was frightened and fell to the ground, his body swollen, and his life may be in danger.

Xiaoshan: Cold, Rainy Weather Affects Sericulture 78

The weather in Xiaoshan had been mild in recent days, and most of the silkworms in the surrounding villages had hatched. Silkworm farmers in Chexiang had begun feeding the silkworms, and most of the early batches had already entered their first molt. However, starting on the 26th, there were three days and nights of heavy rain, and a strong northwest wind suddenly caused the weather to turn cold. Most of the hatched young silkworms froze to death, and the early batches in their first molt mostly stopped eating. The continuous rain also caused the mulberry leaves to be waterlogged, and the silkworms were spitting out yellow water. This year's silkworm season does not look promising. Although the improved breed is more resistant to cold, sick silkworms have been found, reducing the harvest by half. There is little hope for a good harvest this season.

Henan Xinye County Appeals for Disaster Relief by Telegram 79

To the Editors of the Shanghai Shen Bao,

Last year, Xinye County experienced unprecedented flooding, which destroyed not only homes and fields, but also nearly a century of accumulated wealth. The people are suffering from both hunger and drowning, and the situation is dire. Fortunately, we were rescued by philanthropists from all over the world, and we were able to survive last autumn and winter by eating bran and grass. Since the beginning of spring, relief supplies have been exhausted, and there is almost no smoke rising from the chimneys. Throughout the disaster area, not a single chicken or dog can be heard. The trees have been stripped bare, and the walls are empty. Skinny children lean on their emaciated mothers and weep, while starving husbands lie beside the villages, waiting for death. With the gap between the old and new harvests, rice prices are soaring, which is a death sentence for the dying victims. Although an empty stomach can endure for a limited time, the spring breeze cannot alleviate hunger. Our association has no magical powers to raise money, and we are both knowledgeable and capable but are facing difficulties. In our mind's eye, we see corpses dying of starvation, and in our ears, we hear cries of hunger. We are filled with anxiety day and night, and our hearts ache. Although beans and wheat will be harvested soon, the wait is unbearable. This group of people, who are difficult to serve, although born in deep water and bitter cold, will lose their lives in late spring and early summer. Your newspaper is widely circulated both at home and abroad, reaching every corner of the world. Therefore, we dare to represent the victims and appeal to you. Please lend a hand and publish our plea in your newspaper so that philanthropists at home and abroad can understand the urgent need for rescue in Xinye County and generously contribute to save us. If Xinye can reduce the loss of one life, it will increase the vitality of the entire society. The words of the benevolent are more valuable than cash. We implore you with a hundred bows and await your kind response.

Respectfully,

Zhao Guanjun, Chairman of the Xinye County Disaster Relief Association

Open Letter to Workers: The China Labor Association's Open Letter to the National Labor Community

As we commemorate the 51st anniversary of the International Labor Day, we respectfully offer five points to our countrymen: First, the International Labor Day was born out of the struggle of international workers, especially American workers. The outcome of the International Labor Day is the herald of victory for the international workers' movement. As such, the significance of our commemoration of the International Labor Day lies in strengthening the organization and unity of the labor community. Second, we must remember the temporal and spatial context of China when we celebrate the International Labor Day. It is undeniable that in this peak stage of the Chinese national revolution, the promotion of the labor movement is of paramount importance. However, the method of promotion must be in line with the goals of the Chinese national revolution and suitable for the needs of the Chinese labor movement. Therefore, we must not blindly follow others when commemorating Labor Day. We must create a Chinese Labor Day with the spirit of "self-reliance" and use it as a model for the Chinese workers' movement. Third, we must promote the spirit of labor service when commemorating Labor Day. On the negative side, we must eliminate the bad habits of laziness, slackness, despondency, and decadence. On the positive side, we must use the perseverance of hard work, sacrifice, and labor service to increase the production of the nation and cultivate a militarized, artistic, and disciplined lifestyle. Fourth, we must work quickly to catch up with the national salvation movement and prepare for the work of extraordinary times in order to fight for the final survival of the nation. Fifth, the promotion of the labor movement is not only reflected in actions and forms, but also in the creation of spirit and substance. The former depends on the strictness of the organization, while the latter depends on the construction and popularization of labor culture. "Building labor culture" is also the most important mission of commemorating Labor Day. What has been said above are all the goals proclaimed in the outline of our association's work, and they are also the beliefs that we are all striving to achieve. We hope that the national labor community will work together to accomplish the mission of the Chinese Labor Day.

Songhu Garrison Commander Announces End of Martial Law in Shanghai, Post of Martial Law Commander Abolished 81

The Songhu Garrison Headquarters announced: "According to the Military Affairs Commission's telegram, 'The recent student unrest has subsided. Martial law in the Shanghai area can be lifted immediately. The post of martial law commander should also be abolished.' Therefore, on December 24, 1935, Commander Wu declared a partial martial law to maintain local security due to the outbreak of student unrest and the complex situation in the city. On December 26 of the same year, the Military Affairs Commission issued an order to declare martial law immediately and appointed the Songhu Garrison Commander as the Martial Law Commander for the Shanghai area. Former Commander Wu issued orders and announcements to comply, and these have been reported on file. In accordance with the aforementioned reasons, we should comply immediately, declare the lifting of martial law immediately, and abolish the post of Martial Law Commander at the same time. In addition to separate orders and reports for compliance, we hereby announce this for general knowledge. This announcement is issued on April 28, 1936."

Hong Kong National Bank Shanghai Branch Reopens Today, Board of Directors Re-elected, Shanghai Branch Manager Ma Huibi, Unsecured Debts Under 100 Yuan Paid in Cash 82

According to Shen Shi She, the Hong Kong National Commercial and Savings Bank, which suspended business in all its branches on September 16 last year due to a run on the bank, has now had a meeting of creditors and shareholders and decided on a resumption plan. In addition to the Hong Kong head office and the branches in Peiping, Tianjin, Guangzhou, and other cities, which resumed business on March 2nd of this year, the Shanghai branch will also officially resume business today. According to inquiries made by the reporter to the bank yesterday, the Shanghai branch was established in May 1923. Since its closure last year, the ninth shareholders' meeting recently re-elected Li Zuochen as chairman of the board, and Mai Junsheng, Guo Quan, Zhou Huaizhang, Cai Chang, Cai Xing, Huang Weilou, Lin Zhixuan, Ma Yongcan, Wang Guoxuan, Nie Jianting, Li Changli, Xia Congzhou, Lin Zifeng, and Lu Zhongyun as directors. The Hong Kong head office manager is Wang Guoxuan, and the Shanghai branch manager is Ma Huibi. The bank is registered with the Hong Kong government and registered with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, but it has not joined the Bankers Association. The registered capital is HK$5 million, divided into 500,000 shares, each with a par value of HK$10. Of this amount, HK$2,574,100 is divided into 257,410 ordinary shares, which have already been issued. The remaining HK$2,425,900 of capital that has not been issued is divided into two types: Type A preferred shares (60,000 shares, each with a par value of HK$10) and Type B preferred shares (182,590 shares, each with a par value of HK$10). As for the company's handling of claims by unsecured creditors, 50% of Type B preferred shares will be returned. This type of share will be considered as already having the full face value paid. However, any fractions less than one yuan will not be issued as Type B preferred shares. As for unsecured creditors, those with claims not exceeding HK$100 (equivalent to RMB$130) may request repayment in cash.
